[Completed] Server Check and Cash Shop Update on 22nd January 2025


21 Jan 2025

[Completed] Server Check and Cash Shop Update on 22nd January 2025


Dear Maplers,

Please be informed that there will be a scheduled maintenance on 22nd January 2025.
During this period, services undergoing maintenance will be temporarily unavailable.


Game Maintenance
  • Maintenance Period: 22nd January 2025, 0900hrs ~ 1053hrs 1200hrs (GMT+8)
  • Affected Service(s): MapleStorySEA game servers
  • Impact: All MapleStorySEA game servers will be unavailable
    • â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ª Game services for all worlds will not be available during the stipulated time. Kindly log out before this period to avoid disruptions to your gameplay.

    Website Maintenance (Updated 0910hrs)
  • Maintenance Period: 22nd January 2025, 0930hrs ~ 1030hrs (GMT+8)
  • Affected Service(s): MapleStorySEA Passport Website, parts of MapleStorySEA Official Website
  • Impact: MapleStorySEA Passport will be unavailable; Certain media content in official MapleStorySEA website will be unavailable

    Update Preview
  • Cash Shop Update details for 22nd January 2025 can be found here.

    • Known Issues
  • List of known issues, issues scheduled to be fixed and fixed issues can be found here.

    • Thank you.

    - MapleSEA Administrator

    Champion Burning Double Up


    1 + 1 + 1

    25th December 2024, 1000hrs ~ 11th March 2025, 2359hrs



    Available to Level 101+, Zero character who has completed Chapter 2 for Story Quest


    â—What is Champion Double Up?
    Champion Double Up allows you to designate three Champion characters in a World. One of them can be designated as the Champion Leader first.

    Double Up Attendance
    ğŸ”¹ Double Up Attendance can only be performed by the Champion Leader by hunting monsters within the level range.
    ğŸ”¹ Each Champion will receive 2,500 Double Up Coins for each completed attendance. A dedicated Coin Shop is available for each Champion character.
    (7,500 total for each attendance)

    Double Up EXP Points Accumulation
    ğŸ”¹ Double Up EXP Points can only be accumulated by the Champion Leader.
    ğŸ”¹ Every time the Leader hunts a monster within the level range, the non-Leader Champions' Double Up EXP Points will increase (up to 100,000 per week).
    ğŸ”¹ You can log in to your non-Leader Champions to spend Double Up EXP Points and earn EXP.

    Note
    ğŸ”¹ You can only continue in the same World where you initially assigned the Leader.
    ğŸ”¹ The designated Champions can never be changed to another character.
    ğŸ”¹ You can only change your Leader once a week from among your designated Champions.
  • Once understood, select I understand now. Go Assign a leader..

    CHAMPION DOUBLE UP


    IMPORTANT GUIDE

    Setting Leader
    1. Click Set in the Leader Box.


    2. Choose the desired leader character and click SELECT.


    3. You will be shown a confirmation if you want to select the current login world to participate the event.


    4. Type the (Current World)/Proceed.


    5. Click Yes if the desired character selection is final. If not, click No, to change.


    6. After confirming the character, type (IGN)/Proceed.


    Setting Champion
    1. Click Set in the Champion Box.


    2. Choose the desired champion character and click SELECT.


    3. You will be shown a confirmation if you want the selected character to be set as Champion.


    4. After confirming the character, type (IGN)/Proceed.


  • LEADER will have a special skill located in the beginner tab to summon both Champions.


    IMPORTANT NOTE
    â€ƒâ†ª You cannot change the LEADER and CHAMPIONS after assigning them.
    â€ƒâ†ª You cannot set the same character as both LEADER and CHAMPIONS.
    â€ƒâ†ª You can only change the LEADER from either of the selected CHAMPIONS.
    â€ƒâ†ª Hyper Burning Characters CAN be selected.

    General Progression
  • Eliminate level range monsters (-20/+20) with LEADER to gain points for both Champion.
  • up to 100,000 monsters per week which resets after Wednesday 11:59p.m.
  • 1 level range monsters (-20/+20) = 1 Point.
  • Eliminate level range monsters (-20/+20) with CHAMPION will not gain any points.
  • Points obtained by both Champion can be converted into EXP points.
  • EXP Points gained will be based on the character's level.


    Double Up Coin
  • Eliminate 2,000 level range monsters (-20/+20) with LEADER 3 times a week to get up to 7,500 Double Up Coins.
  • Both Champion will obtain its own separate Double Up Coins along with the LEADER.
  • Up to 100,000 level range monsters (-20/+20) can be eliminated by the LEADER per week which resets after Wednesday 11:59p.m.
  • Click the USE button to consume 3,000 Maple Points for DOUBLE UP PASS to catch up with the times you missed.
  • Both LEADER and the 2 CHAMPION will obtain its own Double Up Coins from the DOUBLE UP PASS.

    [Coin Shop] Champion Double Up Coin Shop
  • Champion Double Up Coin Shop ends on 16th March 2025, 2359hrs. (Updated: 24th December 2024, 0007hrs)
  • Both LEADER and the 2 CHAMPION has its own purchase limit that does not affect each other.
  • Item duration, purchase limit, functionality and tradability are as shown in game.

    17 Dec 2024

    CHASER II: New Name Auction Highlight Notes (v238) [Updated 22nd Jan 1726hrs]




    Developer Notes

    Hereâ€™s your chance to win the name youâ€™ve always wantedâ€”the New Name Auction is here!

    The event features two phases: Season 1 - New Name Auction Official Bidding and Season 2 - Character Name Buying/Selling.

    Donâ€™t miss out the New Nameâ€™s Auction and change to a cool and unique name for your character!


    CAUTIONARY NOTES UPON STARTING

    Notes on Trading
  • MapleStory retains ownership of the character name, and the rights to use the name are transferred to the buyer upon completion of the trade.
  • Character names that violate the Name Policy are subject to Admin judgement, and purchasing and using them may result incur penalties based on the Operation Policy.
  • You can only have 1 listing for sale at a time.
  • You can have up to 10 character name trades going on at a time.
  • When you register to sell a name, the registration deposit and a renaming free will be deducted, and the character will immediately take on a new name.
  • The registration deposit will be refunded if the sale is successful, but not if the sale is unsuccessful.
  • The remaining fee cannot be returned regardless of the success of the sale.
  • If the sale is successful, you will receive the sale proceeds minus the sale fee.
  • If the sale is unsuccessful, you can get your character's name back.

    Notes on Names
  • If a name you list for sale is found to be in violation of the Name Policy, the trade may be canceled by the Admin.
  • Names that violate the Name Policy can be restricted from use and forcibly changed.
  • Name change fees and bid deposits used to trade names that violate the Name Policy are non-refundable.
  • Accounts that trade names in violation of the Name Policy will be restricted from future New Name Auctions.

    Notes on Claiming (Changing) Names
  • You cannot change to a name that already exists.
  • You cannot change to a name that contains certain restricted words.
  • Changing a character's name will not change the name on previously crafted items.
  • NPCs registered as statues cannot be renamed.


    CAUTIONARY NOTES WHEN BIDDING

    Trade-Related Cautionary Notes
  • Ownership of character names belongs to MapleStory, and upon successful trade, naming rights are transferred to the buyer.
  • Character names that violate the Name Policy are subject to Admin judgement. Purchasing and using such names may incur penalties based on the Operation Policy.
  • Cancellation due to a change of mind after bidding is not possible. You can rebid at a higher price before the auction ends.
  • A maximum of 4 character name transactions can be conducted simultaneously. This includes both sales and bids, with a limit of 5, including unreceived transactions from sales, bids, and completed deals.
  • Bid deposits and name change fees are deducted in advance when placing a bid, and both are refunded in case of failure.
  • Upon winning, the character name is immediately changed and the previous character name is deleted. Once the character name change is completed, it cannot be reversed.

    Name-Related Cautionary Notes
  • If the bid name is found violate naming policies, the trade may be forcibly canceled.
  • Names violating naming policies may be restricted from use and forcibly changed.
  • Name change fees and bid deposits used in transactions involving names violating policies are non-refundable.
  • Accounts involved in trading names that violate policies may face restrictions on future New Name Auction usage.

    Cautionary Notes for Name Reception (Change) after Winning
  • After receiving the character name, the character cannot change names for one week.
  • The name displayed on items crafted prior to a character name change will not be altered.
  • The names of NPCs registered in the beauty salon will not be changed.


    CAUTIONARY NOTES FOR NAME RECEPTION

    Cautionary Notes for Name Reception
  • After receiving the character name, the character cannot change name through NPC Mister New Name for one week.
  • The name displayed on items crafted prior to a character name change will not be altered.
  • The names of NPCs registered in the beauty salon will not be changed.
  • Regardless of the timing of the character name change, you can receive character names won through a successful bid or return character names you did not win.

    (Updated 22 Jan 2025, 1726hrs)
  • Under the following situation, character name from New Name Auction Season 1 will not be release back to the IGN pool.
    • â€ƒâ†ª The character name is deleted by performing character deletion.
    â€ƒâ†ª The character name is replaced with another character name from New Name Auction.


    Season 1 - New Name Auction Official Bidding

    18th December 2024, (after v238 Patch) ~ 7th January 2025, 2359hrs



    Available to Level 10+, Zero character who has completed Chapter 2 for Story Quest.

  • Selected names will be available for purchase using Maple Points.
  • Starting bid for each Name is 1,000 Maple Points.
  • Everyday at 10:00a.m, new names will be available for bidding.
  • Each Name will be in the Auction for 48 hours for bidding starting from the initial time it is added to the Auction.
  • There is a maximum of 10 Trade slots per MapleID.
  • The Filter Function above can be used to search for more specific name details such as Words Only or Numbers only as well as the length and price of the Name.
  • The auction of a Name ends 2 minutes before the designated auction end time will end randomly between 2 minutes before and 2 minutes after the designated end time, and the highest bid price at the end wins the character Name. (Updated: 24th December 2024, 0000hrs)
  • The New Name Auction is available on a per Maple ID basis.
  • List of available names can be found HERE.

    How to bid
    1. Click on 'New Name Auction Season 1' from the event list or NPC Mister New Name located in main cities, then click the [JOIN] button to enter the New Name Auction.
    2. Search for the desired character name in the search bar on the top left, or find the 'CHARACTER NAME FOR SALE' you like in the search tab.


    3. Write down your desired bid and bid
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªThe first bid(1,000 Maple Points) is unaffected by the Minimum Bid Increment and will be available from 1,000 Maple points. Subsequent bids will be affected by the Minimum Bid Increment.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªWhen bidding, the bid deposit and name change fee are deducted. If the bid is unuccessful, they are returned.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªCancellation is not possible after bidding.
    4. You can check the names currently being bid on by pressing the [ON SALE] button in the 'MY TRADE' tab.


    5. In the 'BID INFORMATION' tab, if the amount you have bid is the highest for that Name, it will be displayed as the WINNING BID. If someone else has bid a higher amount for a character name that has not yet finished its sales period, the 'RE-BID' and 'RETURN BID AMOUNT' buttons will be activated.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªWhen re-bidding, the original bid amount will not be returned, but only the added amount is deducted from your Maple Point balance.


    6. If you win a bid, you can receive the name won in the 'TRANSACTION COMPLETED' button under 'MY TRADE' tab. If you receive the name, the name of the currently logged-in character will be changed immediately and the existing character name will be deleted.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªAfter receiving the character name, the character cannot change their character name through NPC Mister New Name for a week.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªAfter receiving the character name, you can change it to another name that you have won. However, as the previous name cannot be restored once the change is complete, please check the character that will use the name you have won is correct before receiving the name.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªThe name displayed on items previously created by the character whose name you want to change cannot be changed.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªNPCs registered as statues cannot have their name changed.






    Season 2 - Character Name Buying/Selling

    Buying/Selling Period: 8th January 2025, 1000hrs ~ 4th February 2025, 2359hrs

    Registration Buying/Selling Period: 8th January 2025, 1000hrs ~ 31st January 2025, 2359hrs



    Available to Level 10+, Zero character who has completed Chapter 2 for Story Quest.

  • Login to a character to sell the Character Name.
  • A new Name is required to replace the current Name for selling.
  • Each Name will be in the Auction for bidding starting from the time it is added to the Auction.
  • There is a maximum of 10 Trade Slots per MapleID.
  • The Filter Function above can be used to search for more specific name details such as Words Only or Numbers only as well as the length and price of the Name.
  • The auction of a Name ends 2 minutes before the designated auction end time will end randomly between 2 minutes before and 2 minutes after the designated end time, and the highest bid price at the end wins the character Name. (Updated: 24th December 2024, 0000hrs)
  • The New Name Auction is available on a per Maple ID basis.
  • The names and prices of the finished auctions will be changed to 11:59p.m. PM on Tuesday, March 11, 2025 and can be received through the NPC Mister New Name in the village after the event ends.
  • Make sure to use the correct character to receive the auction name.

    How to SELL Names
    1. Click on 'New Name Auction Season 2' from the NPC Mister New Name located in main cities or the event list, then click the [JOIN] button to enter the New Name Auction.
    2. Go to the 'MY TRADE' tab and click the [SELL NAME] button.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªCharacter names that have started selling cannot be cancelled or changed midway.
    3. Enter your desired bid, select a registration time, and enter a new character name to start selling.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªThe minimum bid starts at 50,000 Maple Points, and the registration deposit Name Change Fee of 18,000 Maple Points is deducted at the time of registration.


    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªThere will be Cautionary Notes to read when selling names.






    4. You can check the character names you are selling by clicking the [ON SALE] button in the 'MY TRADE' tab.


    5. When the character name sale is over, you can check the results by clicking the [TRANSACTION COMPLETED] button in the 'MY TRADE' tab. If the registered character name was not sold, you can re-register the sale by paying an additional registration deposit or receive a return of the name.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªThe name change fee is non-refundable regardless of the success of the sale.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªThe registration deposit is refundable if the sale is successful, but not if the sale fails.
    6. You can receive the sales proceeds for the winning character name by clicking the [RECEIVE FUNDS] button in the 'TRANSACTION COMPLETED' tab.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªA 30% sales commission is deducted at the time of payment receipt.



    How to BUY Names
    1. Click on 'New Name Auction' from the event list or NPC Mister New Name located in main cities, then press the [JOIN] button to enter the New Name Auction.
    Search for the desired character name in the search bar on the upper left, or find the 'CHARACTER NAME FOR SALE' you like in the search tab.
    2. Write the desired bid price and bid.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªThe bid price must be higher than the minimum bid unit.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªFor the very first bid(50,000 Maple Points) is unaffected by the Minimum Bid Increment and will be available from 50,000 Maple points. Subsequent bids will be affected by the Minimum Bid Increment.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªBidders must increase their bid by at least the Minimum Bid Increment to bid.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªThere will be Cautionary Notes to read when bidding.






    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªOn a successful bid, bid deposit and name change fee will be deducted first. On a failed bid, everything will be refunded.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªBids cannot be cancelled.


    3. You can check the character names currently being bid on by pressing the [BID IN PROGRESS] button in the 'MY TRADE' tab.


    4. In the 'BID INFORMATION' tab, if the amount you have bid is the highest for that Name, it will be displayed as the WINNING BID. If someone else has bid a higher amount for a character name that has not yet finished its sales period, the 'RE-BID' and 'RETURN BID AMOUNT' buttons will be activated.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªWhen re-bidding, the original bid amount will not be returned, but only the added amount is deducted from your Maple Point balance.


    5. If you win a bid for a character name, you can receive the name with the [TRANSACTION COMPLETED] button in the 'MY TRADE' tab. If you receive the name, the name of the currently logged-in character will be changed immediately and the existing character name will be deleted.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªAfter receiving the character name, the character cannot change the character name through NPC Mister New Name for a week.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªAfter receiving the character name, you can change it to another name that you have won. However, as the previous name cannot be restored once the change is complete, please check the character that will use the name you have won is correct before receiving the name.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªThe name displayed on items previously created by the character whose name you want to change will not be changed.
    â€ƒâ€ƒâ†ªNPCs registered as statues cannot have their name changed

    Scheduled Minor Patch - January 23, 2025


    We will be performing a scheduled minor patch Thursday, January 23, 2025 at 5:00 AM PST (8:00 AM EST / 2:00 PM CET / 12:00 AM AEDT January 24).Â We anticipate the maintenance to last approximatelyÂ 6 hours, concluding around 11:00 AM PST (2:00 PM EST / 8:00 PM CET / 6:00 AM AEDT January 24).

    Times:

    Thursday, January 23, 2025
    PST (UTC -8): 5:00 AM - 11:00 AM
    EST (UTC -5): 8:00 AM - 2:00 PM
    CET (UTC +1): 2:00 PM - 8:00 PM
    AEDT (UTC +11): 12:00 AM - 6:00 AM (January 24)

    • What will be unavailable:
      • All MapleStory game servers.
    • Changes and Updates (Additional Changes TBA):
      • MapleStory will be updated to v.256.5.0.
      • Resolved an issue where Zero characters were unable to upgrade Lazuli/Lapis Type 9 to Genesis Lazuli/Lapis in the Weapon Upgrade UI.
      • Resolved an issue where the dropdown menu in the New Name Auction was blocking the name listings.
      • Resolved an issue where Guardian Angel Slime in Ride or Die would sometimes not reappear after completing the slime door mini-game.
      • Resolved an issue where using a Powerful Rebirth Flame on a Scarlet Shoulder would disconnect the player from the game.
      • Resolved an issue where the Bellamoa Damage Skin (Unit) displayed incorrect units.
      • Resolved an issue where the amount of Maple Points received did not match the amount displayed in the New Name Auction.
        • This minor issue resulted in a difference of 1 Maple Point
      • Resolved an issue where the background in Limbo Phase 1 did not change when switching between Specter A and Specter B.
      • Resolved an issue where the processing buttons were misaligned in the End Trade tab of the New Name Auction.
      • Resolved an issue where the text description was missing from Althea's Weapon details.
      • Resolved an issue where the 'Epic Dungeon: Angler Company' was not being displayed on the Maple Planner.

    Luna Crystal

    • PST (UTC -8): Wednesday, January 8, 2025 12:00 AM - Tuesday, February 4, 2025 11:59 PM
    • CET (UTC +1): Wednesday, January 8, 2025 9:00 AM - Wednesday, February 5, 2025 8:59 AM

    • Luna Crystal
      • Price (1): 3,900 NX
      • Duration: Permanent

    See all the rewards rates for this item here.

    Use the Luna Crystal (available exclusively in Interactive worlds) on a pair of Wonderberry pets to create a stronger buddy to help you out! By combining pets you get from Wisp's Wondrous Wonderberry or the Luna Crystal, you can get higher quality and more powerful 90-day pets!

    Use two Wonder Black pets, which can be obtained from Wisp's Wondrous Wonderberry, and receive either:

    • A Sweet Luna quality Winter Deer, Snow Ram, Winter Snowy, Power XO Bun, Super XO Bun, Magic XO Bun, Baby Hippo, Wolf Pup, and Lion Cub 90-day pet.
    • A chance at a Petite Luna quality Florian, Florence, and Lil Flora 90-day pet.
    • Or the permanent Luna Crystal Key Pet Equipment, which can be used by any of the Petite Luna pets and give the appearance of their normal Pet Equipment!

    You can also combine a Wonder Black and Sweet Luna pet together and receive either:

    • A Dream Luna quality Winter Deer, Snow Ram, Winter Snow, Power XO Bun, Super XO Bun, Magic XO Bun, Baby Hippo, Wolf Pup, and Lion Cub 90-day pet.
    • Better chances at a Petite Luna quality Florian, Florence, and Lil Flora 90-day pet.
    • Or the permanent Luna Crystal Key Pet Equipment!

    Note: The Winter Snowy pet currently has the incorrect in-game name of "Winter Snow" pet. This will be corrected soon in an upcoming update.

    Different quality pets grant different stat boosting skills when equipped as a set, instead of their normal pet set sklls:

    • Sweet Luna (Sweet Luna Skill): 1 pet grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +6. 2 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +14. 3 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +24.
    • Dream Luna (Dream Luna Skill): 1 pet grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +7. 2 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +16. 3 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +27.
    • Petite Luna (Butterfly Garden Skill): Comes with a Meso Magnet skill with a larger area of effect than normal. 1 pet grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +8. 2 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +18. 3 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +36Â and increased item pickup range.
